### [320] [Statistical Parsing for Logical Information Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12170)
*Greg Coppola*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 扩展了量化布尔贝叶斯网络（QBBN），增加了否定/反向推理能力，并开发了自然语言解析器，实现了从自然语言到逻辑形式的完整推理系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决之前QBBN模型的两个主要缺陷：缺乏否定/反向推理能力，以及没有自然语言解析器。旨在构建一个完整的自然语言推理系统，将形式语义学与大规模语言模型相结合。

Method: 1. 推理扩展：在QBBN中增加NEG因子，强制P(x) + P(neg x) = 1，通过反向lambda消息实现逆否推理，完成Prawitz的简单消去规则；2. 语义：提出带类型标记谓词、模态量词的三层表达能力逻辑语言；3. 语法：开发类型槽语法，将句子确定性编译为逻辑形式；4. 架构：LLM预处理，语法解析，LLM重排序，QBBN推理。

Result: 1. 推理引擎处理44/44测试用例，覆盖22种推理模式；2. 语法解析器33/33正确，零歧义；3. LLM处理消歧（95%介词短语附着准确率），但无法直接生成结构化解析（12.4%UAS），证实语法是必要的；4. 整体架构有效整合LLM和形式推理。

Conclusion: 该工作成功将形式语义学与Sutton的"苦涩教训"相协调：LLM消除了形式NLP的标注瓶颈，作为标注器，而QBBN作为验证器，实现了自然语言到逻辑推理的完整管道。

Abstract: In previous work (Coppola, 2024) we introduced the Quantified Boolean Bayesian Network (QBBN), a logical graphical model that implements the forward fragment of natural deduction (Prawitz, 1965) as a probabilistic factor graph. That work left two gaps: no negation/backward reasoning, and no parser for natural language.
  This paper addresses both gaps across inference, semantics, and syntax. For inference, we extend the QBBN with NEG factors enforcing P(x) + P(neg x) = 1, enabling contrapositive reasoning (modus tollens) via backward lambda messages, completing Prawitz's simple elimination rules. The engine handles 44/44 test cases spanning 22 reasoning patterns. For semantics, we present a typed logical language with role-labeled predicates, modal quantifiers, and three tiers of expressiveness following Prawitz: first-order quantification, propositions as arguments, and predicate quantification via lambda abstraction. For syntax, we present a typed slot grammar that deterministically compiles sentences to logical form (33/33 correct, zero ambiguity). LLMs handle disambiguation (95% PP attachment accuracy) but cannot produce structured parses directly (12.4% UAS), confirming grammars are necessary. The architecture: LLM preprocesses, grammar parses, LLM reranks, QBBN infers.
  We argue this reconciles formal semantics with Sutton's "bitter lesson" (2019): LLMs eliminate the annotation bottleneck that killed formal NLP, serving as annotator while the QBBN serves as verifier. Code: https://github.com/gregorycoppola/world

</details>


### [321] [Pedagogically-Inspired Data Synthesis for Language Model Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12172)
*Bowei He,Yankai Chen,Xiaokun Zhang,Linghe Kong,Philip S. Yu,Xue Liu,Chen Ma*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM知识蒸馏方法缺乏教学意识，将知识转移视为一次性数据合成和训练任务，而不是系统化的学习过程。需要借鉴教育原则来改进蒸馏效果。

Method: 提出IOA三阶段框架：1) 知识识别器识别学生模型的知识缺陷；2) 知识组织器通过渐进式课程组织知识传递；3) 知识适配器将表示适配到学生模型的认知能力。融合了布鲁姆掌握学习原则和维果茨基最近发展区理论，创建动态蒸馏过程。

Conclusion: IOA框架通过借鉴教育原则，实现了系统化的知识蒸馏，显著提升了小模型的性能，特别是在复杂推理任务上。这为高效AI系统部署提供了新的教学启发的蒸馏方法。

In this paper, we propose a novel pedagogically-inspired framework for LLM knowledge distillation that draws from fundamental educational principles. Our approach introduces a three-stage pipeline -- Knowledge Identifier, Organizer, and Adapter (IOA) -- that systematically identifies knowledge deficiencies in student models, organizes knowledge delivery through progressive curricula, and adapts representations to match the cognitive capacity of student models. We integrate Bloom's Mastery Learning Principles and Vygotsky's Zone of Proximal Development to create a dynamic distillation process where student models approach teacher model's performance on prerequisite knowledge before advancing, and new knowledge is introduced with controlled, gradual difficulty increments. Extensive experiments using LLaMA-3.1/3.2 and Qwen2.5 as student models demonstrate that IOA achieves significant improvements over baseline distillation methods, with student models retaining 94.7% of teacher performance on DollyEval while using less than 1/10th of the parameters. In this paper, we perform a large-scale anatomical analysis of text prompting in vision-language segmentation, covering 404,796 real prompts across multiple benchmarks. ### [324] [CM2: Reinforcement Learning with Checklist Rewards for Multi-Turn and Multi-Step Agentic Tool Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12268)
*Zhen Zhang,Kaiqiang Song,Xun Wang,Yebowen Hu,Weixiang Yan,Chenyang Zhao,Henry Peng Zou,Haoyun Deng,Sathish Reddy Indurthi,Shujian Liu,Simin Ma,Xiaoyang Wang,Xin Eric Wang,Song Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CM2是一个强化学习框架，通过检查清单奖励替代可验证结果奖励，用于优化多轮多步的工具使用AI代理，在模拟环境中训练并显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实任务中AI代理需要处理多轮用户交互和调用外部工具，但强化学习应用面临挑战：现实目标缺乏可验证奖励、强调开放行为；多轮多步工具使用的RL研究不足；构建可执行工具环境成本高，限制了规模和覆盖范围。

Method: CM2使用检查清单奖励替代可验证结果奖励，将每轮预期行为分解为细粒度二元标准，具有明确证据基础和结构化元数据。采用稀疏奖励分配但密集评估标准的策略，在可扩展的LLM模拟工具环境中训练，避免大型工具集的重工程。

Result: 从8B基础模型开始，在8k示例RL数据集上训练，CM2相比监督微调对应模型在tau^-Bench上提升8点，BFCL-V4上提升10点，ToolSandbox上提升12点。结果匹配甚至优于类似规模的开源基线，包括评判模型。

Conclusion: CM2提供了一个可扩展的配方，用于优化多轮多步工具使用代理，无需依赖可验证奖励，在模拟环境中有效训练并显著提升性能。

Abstract: AI agents are increasingly used to solve real-world tasks by reasoning over multi-turn user interactions and invoking external tools. However, applying reinforcement learning to such settings remains difficult: realistic objectives often lack verifiable rewards and instead emphasize open-ended behaviors; moreover, RL for multi-turn, multi-step agentic tool use is still underexplored; and building and maintaining executable tool environments is costly, limiting scale and coverage. We propose CM2, an RL framework that replaces verifiable outcome rewards with checklist rewards. CM2 decomposes each turn's intended behavior into fine-grained binary criteria with explicit evidence grounding and structured metadata, turning open-ended judging into more stable classification-style decisions. To balance stability and informativeness, our method adopts a strategy of sparse reward assignment but dense evaluation criteria. Training is performed in a scalable LLM-simulated tool environment, avoiding heavy engineering for large tool sets. Experiments show that CM2 consistently improves over supervised fine-tuning. Starting from an 8B Base model and training on an 8k-example RL dataset, CM2 improves over the SFT counterpart by 8 points on tau^-Bench, by 10 points on BFCL-V4, and by 12 points on ToolSandbox. The results match or even outperform similarly sized open-source baselines, including the judging model. CM2 thus provides a scalable recipe for optimizing multi-turn, multi-step tool-using agents without relying on verifiable rewards. Code provided by the open-source community: https://github.com/namezhenzhang/CM2-RLCR-Tool-Agent.

</details>


### [325] [Agentic Test-Time Scaling for WebAgents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12276)
*Nicholas Lee,Lutfi Eren Erdogan,Chris Joseph John,Surya Krishnapillai,Michael W. Mahoney,Kurt Keutzer,Amir Gholami*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CATTS是一种动态分配计算资源的测试时缩放技术，通过投票不确定性来识别真正有争议的决策，从而在长视野多步任务中提高性能并减少计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多步智能体任务中，传统的均匀增加计算资源的方法很快会达到性能饱和，且小错误会在长视野中累积。需要一种更智能的动态计算分配方法来提高效率和性能。

Method: 首先对网络智能体进行推理时缩放的实证研究，发现均匀计算分配的性能饱和问题。然后探索更强的聚合策略，包括基于LLM的仲裁器。发现智能体自身投票分布的不确定性统计量（熵和top-1/top-2边际）与下游成功相关，基于此提出CATTS技术，使用投票不确定性动态分配计算资源。

Result: CATTS在WebArena-Lite和GoBrowse上比React性能提升高达9.1%，同时使用的token数量比均匀缩放少2.3倍，实现了效率提升和可解释的决策规则。

Conclusion: CATTS通过利用投票不确定性动态分配计算资源，在多步智能体任务中实现了更好的性能效率权衡，为长视野任务中的测试时缩放提供了实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Test-time scaling has become a standard way to improve performance and boost reliability of neural network models. However, its behavior on agentic, multi-step tasks remains less well-understood: small per-step errors can compound over long horizons; and we find that naive policies that uniformly increase sampling show diminishing returns. In this work, we present CATTS, a simple technique for dynamically allocating compute for multi-step agents. We first conduct an empirical study of inference-time scaling for web agents. We find that uniformly increasing per-step compute quickly saturates in long-horizon environments. We then investigate stronger aggregation strategies, including an LLM-based Arbiter that can outperform naive voting, but that can overrule high-consensus decisions. We show that uncertainty statistics derived from the agent's own vote distribution (entropy and top-1/top-2 margin) correlate with downstream success and provide a practical signal for dynamic compute allocation. Based on these findings, we introduce Confidence-Aware Test-Time Scaling (CATTS), which uses vote-derived uncertainty to allocate compute only when decisions are genuinely contentious. CATTS improves performance on WebArena-Lite and GoBrowse by up to 9.1% over React while using up to 2.3x fewer tokens than uniform scaling, providing both efficiency gains and an interpretable decision rule.

</details>

### [326] [How to check in continually over 4,000 days on an online learning platform? An empirical experience and a practical solution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11249)
*Jialiang Lin*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 论文提出GILT方法，帮助在线英语学习平台用户克服打卡中断问题，提升学习持续性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究发现82.5%的在线英语学习平台用户无法长期坚持每日打卡，主要原因是动力不足、遗忘、无聊和时间不足。作者作为有4000+天打卡经验的学习者，希望帮助其他用户培养坚持学习的习惯。

Method: 提出GILT方法（具体内容未在摘要中详细说明），这是一种实用的解决方案，基于扇贝英语学习平台的经验，但可应用于其他学习平台。

Result: 作者个人在扇贝平台保持了超过4000天的打卡记录，证明了方法的有效性。GILT方法旨在帮助用户克服打卡中断问题，培养学习毅力。

Conclusion: 基于扇贝平台的经验和GILT方法可以推广到其他学习平台，帮助用户建立持久的学习习惯，克服打卡中断的常见问题。

Abstract: The check-in service is often provided as an incentive system by online learning platforms to help users establish a learning routine and achieve accomplishment. However, according to the questionnaire conducted in this study, 82.5% of users of online English learning platforms that feature a check-in service have failed to maintain the daily check-in behavior for long-term language learning, mainly by reason of demotivation, forgetfulness, boredom, and insufficient time. As a language learner, I have an empirical experience in maintaining a record of over 4,000 daily check-ins on China's leading online English learning platform of Shanbay. In the meantime, I have been constantly exploring a practical solution to help cultivate perseverance for other users to follow through the learning routine. In this paper, I systematically introduce this practical solution, the GILT method, and its instructions. The experience and solution for perseverance development are based on Shanbay, but they can be applied to other learning platforms for different purposes.

</details>


### [327] [Bizarre Love Triangle: Generative AI, Art, and Kitsch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11353)
*Dejan Grba*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文探讨生成式AI艺术中的媚俗现象，分析专业艺术家使用AI创作时产生的五种表达缺陷，以及这些缺陷如何通过艺术界和AI产业的认可而正常化，最终影响AI话语和艺术素养。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在主流文化中引起广泛关注，但无论是业余爱好者还是专业艺术家，在使用AI创作时都容易产生媚俗作品。本文旨在探讨专业艺术家使用AI创作时产生的表达缺陷，分析这些缺陷如何影响AI艺术的质量和艺术界的认知。

Method: 首先介绍数字媚俗和AI艺术的概念，然后回顾生成式AI艺术作品，分析其中五种相互关联的媚俗表达缺陷：1）肤浅地突出或错误地规避生成模型的正式特征；2）对AI的无力批判；3）模仿性；4）未被承认的诗意相似性；5）过度依赖AI作为文化符号。最后讨论这些缺陷如何通过艺术界和AI产业的认可而正常化。

Result: 研究发现专业艺术家在使用生成式AI创作时会产生五种媚俗表达缺陷，这些缺陷通过艺术界对AI艺术的良好评价以及与AI产业的密切关系而被正常化，导致AI话语的污染和艺术素养的可能腐化。

Conclusion: 认识到艺术家对技术文化趋势的盲目接受的不同方面，理解其功能，并预见其意外影响，对于实现AI艺术的相关性和责任感至关重要。这有助于避免AI艺术中的媚俗化倾向，促进更负责任和有意义的AI艺术创作。

Abstract: Generative artificial intelligence (GenAI) has engrossed the mainstream culture, expanded AI's creative user base, and catalyzed economic, legal, and aesthetic issues that stir a lively public debate. Unsurprisingly, GenAI tools proliferate kitsch in the hands of amateurs and hobbyists, but various shortcomings also induce kitsch into a more ambitious, professional artists' production with GenAI. I explore them in this paper. Following the introductory outline of digital kitsch and AI art, I review GenAI artworks that manifest five interrelated types of kitsch-engendering expressive flaws: the superficial foregrounding or faulty circumvention of generative models' formal signatures, the feeble critique of AI, the mimetics, and the unacknowledged poetic similarities, all marked by an overreliance on AI as a cultural signifier. I discuss the normalization of these blunders through GenAI art's good standing within the art world and keen relationship with the AI industry, which contributes to the adulteration of AI discourse and the possible corruption of artistic literacy. In conclusion, I emphasize that recognizing different facets of artists' uncritical embrace of techno-cultural trends, comprehending their functions, and anticipating their unintended effects is crucial for reaching relevance and responsibility in AI art.

</details>


### [328] [The Manifold of the Absolute: Religious Perennialism as Generative Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11368)
*Arthur Juliani*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 该论文使用变分自编码器的数学框架形式化宗教认识论，将宗教传统建模为从共享潜在空间到可观察文化形式的不同生成映射，论证了排他主义、普遍主义和永恒主义三种配置中，永恒主义最能解释跨传统沉思实践的趋同性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机是使用数学框架（变分自编码器）来形式化宗教认识论，为理解不同宗教传统之间的关系提供严谨的分析工具，特别是解释跨宗教传统中沉思实践的趋同现象。

Method: 方法是将宗教传统建模为从共享低维潜在空间到高维可观察文化形式空间的生成映射，定义了三种竞争性生成配置：排他主义、普遍主义、永恒主义，以及可观察空间的混合主义。通过溯因比较分析这些配置的解释力。

Result: 结果表明：排他主义无法简洁解释跨传统沉思趋同；混合主义因组合不同生成过程的输出而产生不连贯产物而失败；普遍主义遭受后验坍塌问题，剥离传统到共同核心会丢弃必要的结构信息。永恒主义配置提供了最佳解释拟合。

Conclusion: 结论是永恒主义框架最能解释宗教现象，其中严格正统性不是文化约束而是结构必要性：恢复潜在源的沉思实践必须与采用其形式作为输入的特定传统相匹配。宗教的统一性如果存在，是真实但无法通过捷径获得的：必须深入而非广泛探索。

Abstract: This paper formalizes religious epistemology through the mathematics of Variational Autoencoders. We model religious traditions as distinct generative mappings from a shared, low-dimensional latent space to the high-dimensional space of observable cultural forms, and define three competing generative configurations corresponding to exclusivism, universalism, and perennialism, alongside syncretism as direct mixing in observable space. Through abductive comparison, we argue that exclusivism cannot parsimoniously account for cross-traditional contemplative convergence, that syncretism fails because combining the outputs of distinct generative processes produces incoherent artifacts, and that universalism suffers from posterior collapse: stripping traditions to a common core discards the structural information necessary for inference. The perennialist configuration provides the best explanatory fit. Within this framework, strict orthodoxy emerges not as a cultural constraint but as a structural necessity: the contemplative practices that recover the latent source must be matched to the specific tradition whose forms they take as input. The unity of religions, if it exists, is real but inaccessible by shortcut: one must go deep rather than wide.

</details>


### [329] [When Visibility Outpaces Verification: Delayed Verification and Narrative Lock-in in Agentic AI Discourse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11412)
*Hanjing Shi,Dominic DiFranzo*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 研究发现社交媒体上关于自主AI的讨论存在"流行度悖论"：高可见度讨论的验证线索出现显著延迟或缺失，导致早期未经证实的说法在证据出现前固化为集体认知偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主AI系统正在重塑人机信任格局，但用户在直接接触系统前，期望已通过社交媒体上的高风险公共讨论被塑造。平台参与信号（如点赞）可能无意中成为"可信度代理"，抑制批判性评估。

Method: 分析两个具有不同互动文化的Reddit社区（r/OpenClaw和r/Moltbook）的纵向数据集，通过可复现的词汇规则操作化验证线索，使用右删失生存分析框架建模"首次验证时间"。

Result: 发现系统性"流行度悖论"：两个子版块中高可见度讨论的验证线索都显著延迟或完全缺失。这种时间滞后创造了"叙事锁定"的关键窗口期，早期未经证实的说法在证据寻求行为出现前固化为集体认知偏见。

Conclusion: 这种"基于可见度的可信度"效应对AI安全有重要影响，提出"认知摩擦"作为设计干预措施，以重新平衡以参与度驱动的平台。

Abstract: Agentic AI systems-autonomous entities capable of independent planning and execution-reshape the landscape of human-AI trust. Long before direct system exposure, user expectations are mediated through high-stakes public discourse on social platforms. However, platform-mediated engagement signals (e.g., upvotes) may inadvertently function as a ``credibility proxy,'' potentially stifling critical evaluation.
  This paper investigates the interplay between social proof and verification timing in online discussions of agentic AI. Analyzing a longitudinal dataset from two distinct Reddit communities with contrasting interaction cultures-r/OpenClaw and r/Moltbook-we operationalize verification cues via reproducible lexical rules and model the ``time-to-first-verification'' using a right-censored survival analysis framework.
  Our findings reveal a systemic ``Popularity Paradox'': high-visibility discussions in both subreddits experience significantly delayed or entirely absent verification cues compared to low-visibility threads. This temporal lag creates a critical window for ``Narrative Lock-in,'' where early, unverified claims crystallize into collective cognitive biases before evidence-seeking behaviors emerge. We discuss the implications of this ``credibility-by-visibility'' effect for AI safety and propose ``epistemic friction'' as a design intervention to rebalance engagement-driven platforms.

</details>


### [330] [Digital Ecosystems: Enabling Collaboration in a Fragmented World](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11707)
*Marc Schmitt*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个多中心数字生态系统框架，通过四类技术集群实现个人、组织、跨组织和全球层面的数字整合，以应对日益碎片化的世界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着地缘政治、组织和技术碎片化加剧，需要建立弹性的数字协作机制。传统集中式平台模式难以适应碎片化、多极化的世界格局，需要新的数字生态系统框架来支持跨境协调和创新。

Method: 开发了一个多中心数字生态系统谱系框架，包含个人、组织、跨组织和全球四个嵌套层次。通过四类技术集群实现整合：人工智能与自动化、区块链信任、联邦数据空间和沉浸式技术。将数字生态系统重新定义为松散耦合参与者的分布式自适应网络。

Result: 提出了一个多层多中心数字生态系统概念框架，展示了如何通过AI赋能的基础设施实现碎片化多极世界中的数字整合。该框架扩展了平台理论，为跨境协调和创新提供了新路径。

Conclusion: 多中心数字生态系统框架为解决碎片化世界中的数字协作挑战提供了新思路。通过分布式、自适应的网络结构和四类关键技术集群，能够实现跨层次的数字整合，为未来的数字生态系统设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: As geopolitical, organizational, and technological fragmentation deepens, resilient digital collaboration becomes imperative. This paper develops a spectrum framework of polycentric digital ecosystems-nested socio-technical systems spanning personal, organizational, inter-organizational, and global layers. Integration across these layers is enabled by four technology clusters: AI and automation, blockchain trust, federated data spaces, and immersive technologies. By redefining digital ecosystems as distributed, adaptive networks of loosely coupled actors, this study outlines new pathways for crossborder coordination and innovation. The framework extends platform theory by introducing a multi-layer conceptualization of polycentric digital ecosystems and demonstrates how AI-enabled infrastructures can be orchestrated to achieve digital integration in a fragmented, multipolar world.

</details>


### [331] [Artificial intelligence is creating a new global linguistic hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12018)
*Giulia Occhini,Kumiko Tanaka-Ishii,Anna Barford,Refael Tikochinski,Songbo Hu,Roi Reichart,Yijie Zhou,Hannah Claus,Ulla Petti,Ivan Vulić,Ramit Debnath,Anna Korhonen*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 该研究分析了全球6003种语言中AI资源的分布情况，发现少数语言主导加剧了前所未有的数字鸿沟，并提出了语言AI准备度指数（EQUATE）来指导更公平的技术扩散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI技术有潜力改变医疗、教育、治理和社会经济公平，但其好处目前集中在少数语言中。全球7000多种语言社区大多缺乏AI访问，面临持续的数字边缘化问题。需要评估语言AI中的系统性不平等。

Method: 1. 对6003种语言的AI资源存在性进行全球纵向分析；2. 对比AI与早期IT技术的扩散模式；3. 引入语言AI准备度指数（EQUATE），从技术、社会经济和基础设施三个维度评估各语言部署AI的准备程度。

Result: 1. 尽管社区努力扩大语言技术覆盖范围，但少数语言的统治地位正在以前所未有的规模加剧不平等，鸿沟呈指数级扩大而非缩小；2. AI扩散呈现独特的炒作驱动模式；3. EQUATE指数识别出有潜力但未充分利用的社区，为加速更公平的语言AI扩散提供框架。

Conclusion: 该研究为向更可持续和公平的语言技术过渡设定了基线，EQUATE指数为优先排序和资源分配提供了实用指导，有助于加速语言AI的更公平扩散。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) has the potential to transform healthcare, education, governance and socioeconomic equity, but its benefits remain concentrated in a small number of languages (Bender, 2019; Blasi et al., 2022; Joshi et al., 2020; Ranathunga and de Silva, 2022; Young, 2015). Language AI - the technologies that underpin widely-used conversational systems such as ChatGPT - could provide major benefits if available in people's native languages, yet most of the world's 7,000+ linguistic communities currently lack access and face persistent digital marginalization. Here we present a global longitudinal analysis of social, economic and infrastructural conditions across languages to assess systemic inequalities in language AI. We first analyze the existence of AI resources for 6003 languages. We find that despite efforts of the community to broaden the reach of language technologies (Bapna et al., 2022; Costa-Jussà et al., 2022), the dominance of a handful of languages is exacerbating disparities on an unprecedented scale, with divides widening exponentially rather than narrowing. Further, we contrast the longitudinal diffusion of AI with that of earlier IT technologies, revealing a distinctive hype-driven pattern of spread. To translate our findings into practical insights and guide prioritization efforts, we introduce the Language AI Readiness Index (EQUATE), which maps the state of technological, socio-economic, and infrastructural prerequisites for AI deployment across languages. The index highlights communities where capacity exists but remains underutilized, and provides a framework for accelerating more equitable diffusion of language AI. Our work contributes to setting the baseline for a transition towards more sustainable and equitable language technologies.

</details>

### [332] [Sample-Free Safety Assessment of Neural Network Controllers via Taylor Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11332)
*Adam Evans,Roberto Armellin*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出一种通过自动域分割和多项式边界技术评估训练神经网络反馈控制器安全性的方法，为安全关键航天应用提供验证保证


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络控制器在复杂场景中有效但缺乏经典控制策略的验证保证，其黑盒特性在安全关键航天应用中引发可信度担忧，限制了实际应用

Method: 将训练好的神经网络嵌入系统动力学方程形成闭环自治系统，通过高阶泰勒多项式近似系统流，构建多项式映射将状态不确定性投影到事件流形，采用自动域分割确保多项式在相关子域中的准确性，利用多项式边界技术严格约束事件值

Result: 该方法能够建立使用神经网络控制器时可能闭环结果的范围边界，支持安全评估和实际任务中的知情操作决策

Conclusion: 通过自动域分割和多项式边界技术，为神经网络反馈控制器提供了可验证的安全评估框架，有助于提升其在安全关键航天应用中的可信度和采用率

Abstract: In recent years, artificial neural networks have been increasingly studied as feedback controllers for guidance problems. While effective in complex scenarios, they lack the verification guarantees found in classical guidance policies. Their black-box nature creates significant concerns regarding trustworthiness, limiting their adoption in safety-critical spaceflight applications. This work addresses this gap by developing a method to assess the safety of a trained neural network feedback controller via automatic domain splitting and polynomial bounding. The methodology involves embedding the trained neural network into the system's dynamical equations, rendering the closed-loop system autonomous. The system flow is then approximated by high-order Taylor polynomials, which are subsequently manipulated to construct polynomial maps that project state uncertainties onto an event manifold. Automatic domain splitting ensures the polynomials are accurate over their relevant subdomains, whilst also allowing an extensive state-space to be analysed efficiently. Utilising polynomial bounding techniques, the resulting event values may be rigorously constrained and analysed within individual subdomains, thereby establishing bounds on the range of possible closed-loop outcomes from using such neural network controllers and supporting safety assessment and informed operational decision-making in real-world missions.

</details>


### [333] [A Unified Estimation--Guidance Framework Based on Bayesian Decision Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11373)
*Liraz Mudrik,Yaakov Oshman*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 基于贝叶斯决策理论，修改完美信息微分博弈制导律(DGL1)以处理状态估计误差，提出符合广义分离定理的随机制导律，使用交互多模型粒子滤波器计算后验概率密度，并利用决策非唯一性优化估计器性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统微分博弈制导律(DGL1)假设完美信息，但实际应用中状态估计存在误差。常见方法隐含假设常规分离定理有效，但这种假设不合理。需要开发能够处理估计误差的随机制导方法。

Method: 1. 基于贝叶斯决策理论修改DGL1制导律；2. 使用交互多模型粒子滤波器从噪声测量中推导博弈状态的后验概率密度函数；3. 当最优决策非唯一时，利用这一特性塑造追踪者轨迹以增强估计器性能；4. 利用基于粒子的贝叶斯成本计算特性实现实时算法。

Result: 提出了符合广义分离定理的随机制导律，通过蒙特卡洛仿真研究验证了整个估计-决策-制导方案的有效性。算法能够处理状态估计误差，并利用决策非唯一性优化估计性能。

Conclusion: 该方法成功解决了微分博弈制导中的状态估计误差问题，提出了符合广义分离定理的随机制导框架，实现了实时可行的算法，并通过仿真验证了其性能优势。

Abstract: Using Bayesian decision theory, we modify the perfect-information, differential game-based guidance law (DGL1) to address the inevitable estimation error occurring when driving this guidance law with a separately-designed state estimator. This yields a stochastic guidance law complying with the generalized separation theorem, as opposed to the common approach, that implicitly, but unjustifiably, assumes the validity of the regular separation theorem. The required posterior probability density function of the game's state is derived from the available noisy measurements using an interacting multiple model particle filter. When the resulting optimal decision turns out to be nonunique, this feature is harnessed to appropriately shape the trajectory of the pursuer so as to enhance its estimator's performance. In addition, certain properties of the particle-based computation of the Bayesian cost are exploited to render the algorithm amenable to real-time implementation. The performance of the entire estimation-decision-guidance scheme is demonstrated using an extensive Monte Carlo simulation study.

</details>


### [334] [Chemo Hydrodynamic Transceivers for the Internet of Bio-Nano Things, Modeling the Joint Propulsion Transmission trade-off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11380)
*Shaojie Zhang,Ozgur B. Akan*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 催化Janus粒子在IoBNT中的统一模型，揭示了外部光控同时驱动分子发射和自推进的耦合效应，发现运动诱导的衰落会显著影响通信可靠性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物纳米物联网需要能够在复杂流体中导航并交换分子信号的移动纳米机器，现有模型通常将移动性和通信解耦，忽略了它们之间的物理化学耦合

Method: 提出化学-流体动力学收发器统一模型，建立包含催化Janus粒子外部光控、分子发射和自推进耦合的随机信道模型，通过数值分析研究可靠性特征

Result: 发现单峰可靠性特征，存在临界驱动水平，超过该水平信噪比会崩溃；最佳控制水平与链路距离近似线性相关；主动运动噪声被忽略时，误码率会被低估数个数量级

Conclusion: 研究结果为移动感知的IoBNT协议设计和纳米机器人集群的闭环控制提供了物理层指导，强调了考虑主动运动噪声的重要性

Abstract: The Internet of Bio-Nano Things (IoBNT) requires mobile nanomachines that navigate complex fluids while exchanging molecular signals under external supervision. We introduce the chemo-hydrodynamic transceiver, a unified model for catalytic Janus particles in which an external optical control simultaneously drives molecular emission and active self-propulsion. Unlike common abstractions that decouple mobility and communication, we derive a stochastic channel model that captures their physicochemical coupling and shows that actuation-induced distance jitter can dominate the received-signal variance, yielding a fundamental trade-off: stronger actuation increases emission but can sharply reduce reliability through motion-induced fading. Numerical results reveal a unimodal reliability profile with a critical actuation level beyond which the signal-to-noise ratio collapses, and an optimal control level that scales approximately linearly with link distance. Compared with Brownian-mobility baselines, the model exposes a pronounced estimation gap: neglecting active motility noise can underestimate the bit error probability by orders of magnitude. These findings provide physical-layer guidelines for mobility-aware IoBNT protocol design and closed-loop control of nanorobotic swarms.

</details>


### [335] [Power Margin Ratio -- A Large-Signal System Strength Metric for Inverter-Based Resources-Dominated Power Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11429)
*Zitian Qiu,Yunjie Gu*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的系统强度评估指标PMR（功率裕度比），用于评估多馈入电力系统中逆变器的大信号系统强度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着逆变器在电力系统中的渗透率增加，系统强度下降。传统的短路比（SCR）指标无法准确评估逆变器在不同扰动下的系统强度，特别是大信号扰动下的强度评估。

Method: 提出功率裕度比（PMR）作为大信号系统强度评估指标，定义为逆变器在不引起系统不稳定情况下能注入的最大功率与其额定功率之比。通过改进的潮流计算算法获得PMR，并从动力系统理论角度建立其理论基础。

Result: PMR在单机无穷大系统中与SCR相同，但在多馈入系统中表现出优势。综合案例研究验证了PMR能从静态角度有效揭示大信号系统强度。

Conclusion: PMR是一种控制类型相关的系统强度评估指标，能更准确地评估多馈入电力系统中逆变器的大信号系统强度，为系统规划和运行提供更好的指导。

Abstract: As the growing penetration of inverter-based resources (IBRs) in modern power systems, the system strength is decreasing. Due to the inherent difference in short-circuit capacity contributions of synchronous generators and inverters, the short-circuit ratio is not a one-size-fit-all metric to assess the system strength. Following the distinct dynamic behavior of the IBR in small- and large-signal disturbance, the system strength is separated accordingly. To address the large-signal system strength assessment, a control type-dependent metric, Power Margin Ratio (PMR), is proposed in this paper. PMR is defined as the ratio between the maximum power that can be injected to the system without causing any instability and the nominal power of the IBR. It can be obtained via power flow calculation with a modified algorithm. The theoretical foundation of PMR is established from the viewpoint of dynamical systems. PMR is identical to SCR for the single-plant-infinite-bus system, while presents advancement for multi-infeed power systems. Comprehensive case studies and discussions have validated that PMR reveals the large-signal system strength from a static perspective.

</details>


### [336] [Non-Trivial Consensus on Directed Matrix-Weighted Networks with Cooperative and Antagonistic Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11822)
*Tianmu Niu,Bing Mao,Xiaoqun Wu,Tingwen Huang*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文研究了有向符号矩阵加权网络中的非平凡一致性问题，提出了一种在合作与对抗多维交互群体中实现共识的系统方法，突破了以往认为只有完全合作群体才能达成共识的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有研究关注二分一致性和平凡一致性，但符号矩阵加权网络中的非平凡一致性问题尚未得到充分探索。本文旨在解决在同时存在合作与对抗多维交互的群体中实现共识的挑战。

Method: 首先证明了有向符号矩阵加权网络中接地拉普拉斯矩阵的特征值具有正实部，确保系统状态收敛到符号矩阵加权拉普拉斯矩阵的零空间。然后提出系统方法：策略性选择信息代理、精心设计外部信号、精确确定耦合项，并推导耦合系数的下界。

Result: 算法在更宽松的连通性条件下工作，不要求网络结构平衡或不平衡，非平凡一致状态可按需预设。对于无向网络，耦合系数条件比有向情况更宽松。进一步研究了切换拓扑下的非平凡一致性，提出了切换网络收敛的必要条件。

Conclusion: 本文证明了同时存在合作与对抗多维交互的群体能够实现共识，突破了以往认为只有完全合作群体才能达成共识的限制，为符号矩阵加权网络中的非平凡一致性提供了系统解决方案。

Abstract: This paper investigates the non-trivial consensus problem on directed signed matrix-weighted networks\textemdash a novel convergence state that has remained largely unexplored despite prior studies on bipartite consensus and trivial consensus. Notably, we first prove that for directed signed matrix-weighted networks, every eigenvalue of the grounded Laplacians has positive real part under certain conditions. This key finding ensures the global asymptotic convergence of systems states to the null spaces of signed matrix-weighted Laplacians, providing a foundational tool for analyzing dynamics on rooted signed matrix-weighted networks. To achieve non-trivial consensus, we propose a systematic approach involving the strategic selection of informed agents, careful design of external signals, and precise determination of coupling terms. Crucially, we derive the lower bounds of the coupling coefficients. Our consensus algorithm operates under milder connectivity conditions, and does not impose restrictions on whether the network is structurally balanced or unbalanced. Moreover, the non-trivial consensus state can be preset arbitrarily as needed. We also carry out the above analysis for undirected networks, with more relaxed conditions on the coupling coefficients comparing to the directed case. This paper further studies non-trivial consensus with switching topologies, and propose the necessary condition for the convergence of switching networks. The work in this paper demonstrates that groups with both cooperative and antagonistic multi-dimensional interactions can achieve consensus, which was previously deemed exclusive to fully cooperative groups.

</details>


### [337] [A day-ahead market model for power systems: benchmarking and security implications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11842)
*Andrej Stankovski,Blazhe Gjorgiev,James Ciyu Qin,Giovanni Sansavini*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 市场调度相比最优潮流调度会导致安全风险被低估，未满足需求增加高达80%，需要运营商重新配置备用容量和规划策略


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统电力系统安全评估使用最优潮流(OPF)调度，但OPF基于成本最小化，忽略了市场参与者的复杂互动，可能导致系统安全性被高估

Method: 提出基于社会福利的日前市场出清机制，使用Cascades级联停电分析框架，在IEEE-118节点系统（包含三个独立控制区）上进行分析

Result: 市场调度相比OPF调度导致未满足需求增加高达80%，表明传统OPF方法会高估系统安全性

Conclusion: 运营商可以利用这些信息合理配置备用容量并制定高效的扩展规划策略，以更准确地评估系统安全风险

Abstract: Power system security assessments, e.g. via cascading outage models, often use operational set-points based on optimal power flow (OPF) dispatch. However, driven by cost minimization, OPF provides an ideal, albeit unrealistic, clearing of the generating units, disregarding the complex interactions among market participants. The security of the system, therefore, may be overestimated. To address this gap, we introduce a market model with a social-welfare-based day-ahead market clearing mechanism. The security implications are analyzed via Cascades, a cascading outage analysis framework. We apply this framework to the IEEE-118 bus system with three independent control zones. The results show that market dispatch leads to an increase in demand not served of up to 80% higher than OPF, highlighting a security overestimation. Operators can use this information to properly allocate reserves and perform efficient expansion planning strategies.

</details>


### [338] [Gradient-Based Adaptive Prediction and Control for Nonlinear Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11899)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非线性随机动力系统的自适应预测与控制问题，特别是在弱凸性条件下，这能涵盖控制与机器学习中广泛使用的非线性模型（如饱和函数、激活函数等），且无需持续激励条件，更具实际应用价值。

Method: 提出梯度基自适应预测器，基于弱凸性预测损失函数设计自适应算法，在非线性最小相位条件和非线性项线性增长约束下，建立闭环控制误差的收敛速率分析。

Result: 证明了所提自适应预测器的全局收敛性，并给出了渐近性能的显式收敛速率；在非线性最小相位条件下，建立了闭环控制误差的收敛速率；在实际司法量刑数据集上验证了自适应预测算法的有效性，并通过数值仿真评估了自适应控制性能。

Conclusion: 该研究为非线性随机动力系统的自适应预测与控制提供了理论保证，弱凸性条件扩展了适用模型范围，无需持续激励增强了实用性，在实际数据集上的验证证明了方法的有效性。

Abstract: This paper investigates gradient-based adaptive prediction and control for nonlinear stochastic dynamical systems under a weak convexity condition on the prediction-based loss. This condition accommodates a broad range of nonlinear models in control and machine learning such as saturation functions, sigmoid, ReLU and tanh activation functions, and standard classification models. Without requiring any persistent excitation of the data, we establish global convergence of the proposed adaptive predictor and derive explicit rates for its asymptotic performance. Furthermore, under a classical nonlinear minimum-phase condition and with a linear growth bound on the nonlinearities, we establish the convergence rate of the resulting closed-loop control error. Finally, we demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed adaptive prediction algorithm on a real-world judicial sentencing dataset. The adaptive control performance will also be evaluated via a numerical simulation.

### [339] [Adaptive Behavioral Predictive Control: State-Free Regulation Without Hankel Weights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12016)
*Tam W. Nguyen*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出自适应行为预测控制(ABPC)框架，基于流数据在线识别LPV-ARX预测器，通过核递归最小二乘法实现，避免批量Hankel构造和迭代优化，在Hammerstein和NARX系统上验证性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统预测控制方法通常需要批量数据处理和迭代优化，计算复杂度高。本文旨在开发一种基于流数据的自适应预测控制框架，提高计算效率，同时通过非线性核字典增强模型表达能力。

Method: 采用间接自适应预测控制框架，在线识别LPV-ARX预测器（使用核递归最小二乘法），计算有限时域内的闭式预测控制序列，避免批量Hankel构造和迭代优化，通过非线性核字典扩展行为公式的表达能力。

Result: 在Hammerstein和NARX系统上的数值研究表明，当字典与系统类别匹配时，ABPC表现出有效性能，同时揭示了条件数和特征选择对性能的影响。框架强调数值模拟、计算可行性和可复现性。

Conclusion: ABPC为基于流数据的自适应预测控制提供了计算高效的框架，通过在线识别和闭式控制序列计算，避免了传统方法的计算负担，同时通过核字典扩展了非线性系统的建模能力。

Abstract: This paper presents adaptive behavioral predictive control (ABPC), an indirect adaptive predictive control framework operating on streaming data. An LPV--ARX predictor is identified online via kernel--recursive least squares and used to compute closed-form predictive control sequences over a finite horizon, avoiding batch Hankel constructions and iterative optimization. Nonlinear kernel dictionaries extend model expressiveness within a behavioral formulation. Numerical studies on Hammerstein and NARX systems demonstrate effective performance when the dictionary aligns with the plant class and highlight conditioning and feature-selection effects. The paper emphasizes numerical simulation, computational feasibility, and reproducibility.

### [340] [Equivalent Circuit Modeling of Grid-Forming Inverters in (Sub)-Transient Time-Frame](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12202)
*Ambuj Gupta,Balarko Chaudhuri,Mark O'Malley*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种系统方法来量化黑盒电网形成逆变器的有效阻抗，通过频域导纳图分析，揭示了GFM在滤波器电容处而非开关处维持恒定电压的特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前电网形成逆变器的定义要求其在暂态期间维持近乎恒定的内部电压相量，但现有规范未明确定义内部电压源的位置，且缺乏系统方法来量化黑盒GFM模型的有效阻抗。

Method: 首先比较理想电压源与GFM的暂态响应，揭示GFM在滤波器电容处维持恒定电压的特性；然后提出基于频域导纳图的系统方法来量化黑盒GFM模型的有效阻抗。

Result: 使用NREL开发的PSCAD标准GFM模型验证，证明GFM的等效阻抗模型能够合理准确地捕捉暂态响应和静态电压稳定性极限。

Conclusion: 该研究为量化电网形成逆变器的有效阻抗提供了系统方法，澄清了GFM在滤波器电容处维持恒定电压的物理本质，有助于更准确地评估GFM的暂态性能和稳定性。

Abstract: The widely accepted definition of grid-forming (GFM) inverter states that it should behave as a (nearly) constant voltage source behind an impedance by maintaining a (nearly) constant internal voltage phasor in the sub-transient to transient time frame. Some system operators further mandate permissible ranges for this effective impedance. However, these specifications do not clearly define the location of the internal voltage source, and no systematic method exists to quantify its effective impedance for a black-box GFM model. To address this, we first compare the transient responses of an ideal voltage source and a GFM to show that an idealistic GFM maintains a (nearly) constant voltage across the filter capacitor, rather than at the inverter switches. Then we propose a systematic method to quantify the effective impedance of a GFM from its black-box model using frequency-domain admittance plots. Using standard PSCAD GFM models developed by NREL, we demonstrate that the GFM's equivalent impedance model captures the sub-transient response and static voltage stability limit reasonably accurately.

</details>

### [341] [Liquidation Dynamics in DeFi and the Role of Transaction Fees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12104)
*Agathe Sadeghi,Zachary Feinstein*

Main category: q-fin.MF

TL;DR: CPMM交易费用可作为内生安全参数，防止清算操纵攻击，而不仅仅是减少攻击者利润


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化金融中抵押品清算机制容易受到价格操纵和MEV攻击，特别是当现货预言机来自恒定乘积做市商时

Method: 通过动态规划建立利润最大化清算者的最优清算策略模型，明确建模预言机可提取价值，推导闭式清算边界

Result: CPMM交易费用是关键安全参数，不仅能减少攻击者利润，还能使操纵攻击变得无利可图

Conclusion: CPMM交易费用具有双重作用：补偿流动性提供者和内生地增强预言机抗操纵能力，无需时间加权平均或中值化延迟

Abstract: Liquidation of collateral are the primary safeguard for solvency of lending protocols in decentralized finance. However, the mechanics of liquidations expose these protocols to predatory price manipulations and other forms of Maximal Extractable Value (MEV). In this paper, we characterize the optimal liquidation strategy, via a dynamic program, from the perspective of a profit-maximizing liquidator when the spot oracle is given by a Constant Product Market Maker (CPMM). We explicitly model Oracle Extractable Value (OEV) where liquidators manipulate the CPMM with sandwich attacks to trigger profitable liquidation events. We derive closed-form liquidation bounds and prove that CPMM transaction fees act as a critical security parameter. Crucially, we demonstrate that fees do not merely reduce attacker profits, but can make such manipulations unprofitable for an attacker. Our findings suggest that CPMM transaction fees serve a dual purpose: compensating liquidity providers and endogenously hardening CPMM oracles against manipulation without the latency of time-weighted averages or medianization.

</details>
